But this has no linear term in A. Not enough.

**Candidate 46:** `A^2*c0 + A^2*c1/(A+c2)^2 + A*c3/(A+c4) + c5 + c6*cos(c7*log(A*c8+1))`

Set c0=0, c1=0, c5=0: `A*c3/(A+c4) + c6*cos(c7*log(A*c8+1))`
A*c3/(A+c4) is not linear in A unless c4=0, giving c3. That's just a constant. Not enough.

Actually wait - we could set c4 to be very... no, it needs to be exact. If c4=0, A*c3/A = c3, a constant. Can't get a linear term.

So **Candidate 23** is a clear match.

[MATCH FOUND]

**Candidate 23** matches the GT. Setting:
- c0 = 0 (eliminates the rational term)
- c2 = 1, c3 = -0.19494 (gives the linear term -0.19494*A)
- c4 = 0 (eliminates constant)
- c5 = 0.24819, c6 = 1, c7 = 1 (gives 0.24819*cos(log(A+1)))

This yields exactly `-0.19494*A + 0.24819*cos(log(A+1))`, matching the GT.
